    Show basic use of slamÂ¶

    # Authors: Guillaume Auzias <guillaume.auzias@univ-amu.fr>

# License: MIT
# sphinx_gallery_thumbnail_number = 2

    This script shows examples of basic functionalities offered by SLAM. Some (most) of these are actually inherited from Trimesh

    import numpy as np
import trimesh
import slam.io as sio

    Load a mesh stored on the disc as a gifti file

    mesh = sio.load_mesh("../examples/data/example_mesh.gii")

    access mesh edges

    mesh.edges

    array([[   0, 1488],
       [1488, 1506],
       [1506,    0],
       ...,
       [2318, 2319],
       [2319, 2320],
       [2320, 2318]], shape=(13956, 2))

    access mesh faces

    mesh.faces

    TrackedArray([[   0, 1488, 1506],
              [   0, 1506,  656],
              [   0,  656,  659],
              ...,
              [2316, 2324, 2317],
              [2316, 2317, 2318],
              [2318, 2319, 2320]], shape=(4652, 3))

    access mesh vertices

    mesh.vertices

    TrackedArray([[ -3.57061982,  -4.15675116, -17.94052696],
              [ -4.21303892,  -2.84670091, -18.23071289],
              [  1.2885381 , -11.84370995, -15.82085609],
              ...,
              [ -5.71436596,   9.90463257,  19.29592133],
              [ -5.29037666,   9.60190868,  20.25637817],
              [ -4.34501886,  12.83836937,  19.65690804]], shape=(2328, 3))

    access mesh edges

    mesh.edges

    array([[   0, 1488],
       [1488, 1506],
       [1506,    0],
       ...,
       [2318, 2319],
       [2319, 2320],
       [2320, 2318]], shape=(13956, 2))

    whatâs the area of the mesh

    print("mesh.area=", mesh.area)

    mesh.area= 6436.883745975947

    mesh.area_faces

    array([1.03160007, 0.69458893, 0.64635087, ..., 0.6087503 , 0.61997348,
       1.40925126], shape=(4652,))

    mesh.voxelized(2)

    <trimesh.VoxelGrid(np.int64(14), np.int64(36), np.int64(23))>

    boundary of the mesh or list of faces this functionnality requires to install the optional package shapely mesh.outline()

    the convex hull is another Trimesh object that is available as a property lets compare the volume of our mesh with the volume of its convex hull

    np.divide(mesh.volume, mesh.convex_hull.volume)

    np.float64(0.7994007398058253)

    since the mesh is watertight, it means there is a volumetric center of mass which we can set as the origin for our mesh

    mesh.vertices -= mesh.center_mass

    whatâs the moment of inertia for the mesh?

    if there are multiple bodies in the mesh we can split the mesh by connected components of face adjacency since this example mesh is a single watertight body we get a list of one mesh mesh.split()

    find groups of coplanar adjacent faces

    facets = mesh.facets

    bounding spheres and bounding cylinders of meshes are also available, and will be the minimum volume version of each except in certain degenerate cases, where they will be no worse than a least squares fit version of the primitive.

    print(
    mesh.bounding_box_oriented.volume,
    mesh.bounding_cylinder.volume,
    mesh.bounding_sphere.volume,
)
